Source Code

This is a reconstruction of the AGC program Luminary 99 Rev 0. It was the second release of the Lunar Module flight software targeted for use in Apollo 11, after Luminary 97. A bug (which had been around since at least Apollo 10, Luminary 69) was discovered in Rev 0 shortly before the Apollo 11 flight, resulting in a last minute revision into Rev 1, which is what actually flew rather than the Rev 0 presented here. A hardcopy of Rev 0 is known to exist — it belonged to AGC developer Allan Klumpp for many years — but unfortunately the Virtual AGC Project has not had access to that hardcopy. Thus the code you see here had been reconstructed (we believe accurately) rather than transcribed. The first step of the reconstruction of the Rev 0 source code was the transcription of the Rev 1 source code from a hardcopy in the MIT Museum collection. The process of reverting the active portion of the source code (i.e., other than program comments) from Rev 1 to Rev 0 was very minor, consisting only of moving the position of the STARTSB1 label in FRESH START AND RESTART. Allan had previously given us the checksums of the memory banks of Rev 0, and we have verified the program presented here has checksums identical to all banks of Allan's listing of Rev 0. The notations on Allan's Rev 0 program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 099 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-051

A single program comment is known to differ between Rev 0 and Rev 1, but these are harder to reconstruct and verify than changes to the active portion of the code. Thus it is possible that there are additional differences between the program comments in Rev 0 and Rev 1 that are unknown to us, and therefore are not reflected in the code presented here.

016918,000059:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016919,000060:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
016920,000061:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
016921,000062:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016922,000063: 
016923,000064:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
016924,000065: 
016925,000066:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016926,000067:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016927,000068:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016928,000069:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016929,000070: 
016930,000071:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016931,000072:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016932,000073:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016933,000074:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016934,000075:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016935,000076: 
016936,000077:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016937,000078:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016938,000079:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016939,000080:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
016940,000081: 
016941,000082:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
016942,000083:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
016943,000084:

Ramón Alonso, one of the original AGC developers, provides a little more insight: Apparently, nobody had yet arrived at any kind of software requirements for the AGC's user interface when the desire arose within the Instrumentation Laboratory to set up a demo guidance-computer unit with which to impress visitors to the lab. Of course, this demo would have to do something, if it was going to be at all impressive, and to do something it would need some software. In short order, some of the coders threw together a demo program, inventing and using the verb/noun user-interface concept (in the whimsical fashion seen in much of this code), but without any idea that the verb/noun concept would somehow survive into the flight software. As time passed, and more and more people became familiar with the demo, nobody got around to inventing an improvement for the user interface, so the coders simply built it into the flight software without any specific requirements to do so.

However, that does not mean that the verb/noun interface was universally beloved. Ramón says that many objections were received from naysayers, such as "it's not scientific", "it's not dignified", or even "astronauts won't understand it". Even though the coders of the demo hadn't seriously intended the verb/noun interface to be used in any permanent way, it became a kind of devilish game to counter these objections with (perhaps) sophistic arguments as to why the interface was really a good one. In the end, the coders won. I don't know whether they were elated or dismayed by this victory.

The astronauts, of course, could understand the interface, but they did not like it. Most of them really wanted an interface much more like that they had used in aircraft: i.e., lots of dials and switches. Dave Scott is the the only astronaut I'm aware of who had kind words for it (or for the AGC in general), though we are told that Jim McDivitt wasn't necessary completely hostile to it.

—Ron Burkey, 07/2009

016979,000120:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES -
016980,000121: 
016981,000122:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016982,000123:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016983,000124:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016984,000125:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016985,000126:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016986,000127: 
016987,000128:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016988,000129:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
016989,000130:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016990,000131:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016991,000132: 
016992,000133:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016993,000134:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016994,000135:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016995,000136:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
016996,000137:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016997,000138: 
016998,000139:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
016999,000140: 
017000,000141:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
017001,000142:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
017002,000143:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 391 

017004,000145:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
017005,000146:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
017006,000147:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
017007,000148:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
017008,000149:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
017009,000150:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
017010,000151:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
017011,000152:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
017012,000153:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
017013,000154:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
017014,000155: 
017015,000156:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
017016,000157:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
017017,000158:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017018,000159: 
017019,000160:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
017020,000161: 
017021,000162:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
017022,000163:                                                                                                  #        IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
017023,000164:                                                                                                  #        ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
017024,000165: 
017025,000166:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
017026,000167:                                                                                                  #        IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
017027,000168:                                                                                                  #        (WITH OCTAL 01501).
017028,000169:                                                                                                  #        IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
017029,000170:                                                                                                  #        CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
017030,000171:                                                                                                  #                1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
017031,000172:                                                                                                  #                2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
017032,000173: 
017033,000174:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
017034,000175:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
017035,000176: 
017036,000177:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
017037,000178: 
017038,000179:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
017039,000180:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL). :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
017040,000181:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
017041,000182:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
017042,000183: 
017043,000184:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION -
017044,000185: 
017045,000186:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
017046,000187:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
017047,000188:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
017048,000189:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
017049,000190: 
017050,000191:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 392 

017052,000193:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
017053,000194: 
017054,000195:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST -
017055,000196: 
017056,000197:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
017057,000198:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
017058,000199: 
017059,000200:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
017060,000201:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
017061,000202:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
017062,000203:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
017063,000204: 
017064,000205:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
017065,000206:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
017066,000207: 
017067,000208:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
017068,000209:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
017069,000210:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
017070,000211:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
017071,000212: 
017072,000213:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
017073,000214:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
017074,000215: 
017075,000216:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
017076,000217:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
017077,000218: 
017078,000219:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
017079,000220: 
017080,000221:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
017081,000222:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
017082,000223:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
017083,000224:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017084,000225: 
017085,000226:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
017086,000227:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017087,000228: 
017088,000229:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
017089,000230:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.

2003 RSB — The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism. 

017272,000413: 
017273,000414:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
017274,000415:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
017275,000416:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
017276,000417:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
017277,000418:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
017278,000419:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
017279,000420: 
017280,000421:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
017281,000422:                                                                                                  #  MD1   MD2                             (MAJOR MODE)
017282,000423:                                                                                                  #  VD1   VD2 (VERB)      ND1     ND2     (NOUN)
017283,000424:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  R1D2    R1D3    R1D4    R1D5    (R1)
017284,000425:                                                                                                  #  R2D1  R2D2    R2D3    R2D4    R2D5    (R2)
017285,000426:                                                                                                  #  R3D1  R3D2    R3D3    R3D4    R3D5    (R3)
017286,000427: 
017287,000428:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
017288,000429: 
017289,000430:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
017290,000431:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24              R2D2    10
017291,000432:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23              R2D3     7
017292,000433:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22              R2D4     6
017293,000434:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21              R2D5     5
017294,000435:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20              R3D1     4
017295,000436:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16              R3D2     3
017296,000437:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15              R3D3     2
017297,000438:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14              R3D4     1
017298,000439:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13              R3D5     0
017299,000440:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
017300,000441: 
017301,000442:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
017302,000443: 
017303,000444:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB                RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
017304,000445:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
017305,000446:                                                                                                  #  10            1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
017306,000447:                                                                                                  #  9             1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
017307,000448:                                                                                                  #  8             1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
017308,000449:                                                                                                  #  7             1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 397 

017310,000451:                                                                                                  #  6             0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
017311,000452:                                                                                                  #  5             0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
017312,000453:                                                                                                  #  4             0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
017313,000454:                                                                                                  #  3             0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
017314,000455:                                                                                                  #  2             0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
017315,000456:                                                                                                  #  1             0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
017316,000457:                                                                                                  #  0             0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
017317,000458:                                                                                                  #                0000        NO RELAYWORD
017318,000459: 
017319,000460:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
017320,000461: 
017321,000462:                                                                                                  #  BLANK 00000
017322,000463:                                                                                                  #  0     10101
017323,000464:                                                                                                  #  1     00011
017324,000465:                                                                                                  #  2     11001
017325,000466:                                                                                                  #  3     11011
017326,000467:                                                                                                  #  4     01111
017327,000468:                                                                                                  #  5     11110
017328,000469:                                                                                                  #  6     11100
017329,000470:                                                                                                  #  7     10011
017330,000471:                                                                                                  #  8     11101
017331,000472:                                                                                                  #  9     11111
017332,000473: 
017333,000474:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
017334,000475: 
017335,000476:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
017336,000477:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
017337,000478:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11

Page 413 

018030,001171:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
018031,001172: 
018032,001173:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
018033,001174:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
018034,001175:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
018035,001176:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
018036,001177:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
018037,001178: 
018038,001179:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
018039,001180:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
018040,001181: 
018041,001182:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
018042,001183: 
018043,001184:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
018044,001185:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
018045,001186:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
018046,001187: 
018047,001188:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
018048,001189:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
018049,001190:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018050,001191:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
018051,001192:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018052,001193:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
018053,001194: 
018054,001195:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
018055,001196:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
018056,001197:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
018057,001198:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
018058,001199:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
018059,001200: 
018060,001201:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
018061,001202:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
018062,001203: 
018063,001204:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
018064,001205: 
018065,001206:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
018066,001207:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
018067,001208:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018068,001209:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
018069,001210:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018070,001211: 
018071,001212:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
018072,001213:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
018073,001214:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
018074,001215: 
018075,001216:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
018076,001217:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
018077,001218: 
018078,001219:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
018079,001220:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
018080,001221:

Page 437 

019193,002334:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
019194,002335:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
019195,002336:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
019196,002337:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
019197,002338:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
019198,002339: 
019199,002340:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
019200,002341:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
019201,002342:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
019202,002343:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
019203,002344:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
019204,002345:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
019205,002346:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
019206,002347: 
019207,002348:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
019208,002349:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019209,002350:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019210,002351: 
019211,002352:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
019212,002353:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
019213,002354: 
019214,002355:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
019215,002356:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
019216,002357: 
019217,002358:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW
019218,002359: 
019219,002360: 41,3230                                           SETLOC   ENDRUTIN                              
019220,002361:

019222,002363: 41,3230           43237        MONITOR            CS       BIT15/14                              
019223,002364: 41,3231           71017                           MASK     NOUNCADR                              
019224,002365: 41,3232           54155        MONIT1             TS       MPAC       +1                         #  TEMP STORAGE

019343,002484:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
019344,002485:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
019345,002486:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
019346,002487:                                                                                                  #  
019347,002488:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
019348,002489: 
019349,002490:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
019350,002491:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
019351,002492:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
019352,002493: 
019353,002494:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
019354,002495:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
019355,002496:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
019356,002497: 
019357,002498: 41,3353           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
019358,002499: 41,3354           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
019359,002500: 41,3355           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
019360,002501: 41,3356           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
019361,002502: 41,3357           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
019362,002503: 41,3360           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
019363,002504: 41,3361           03363                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
019364,002505: 41,3362           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

019779,002920:

Page 450 

019781,002922: 
019782,002923:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019783,002924: 
019784,002925:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019785,002926: 
019786,002927:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019787,002928:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019788,002929:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019789,002930:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019790,002931: 
019791,002932:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019792,002933:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019793,002934:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019794,002935: 
019795,002936:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019796,002937:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019797,002938:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019798,002939:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019799,002940:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019800,002941:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019801,002942:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019802,002943:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
019803,002944:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST. THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019804,002945:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019805,002946:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019806,002947: 
019807,002948: 40,3461           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019808,002949: 40,3462           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019809,002950: 40,3463           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019810,002951: 40,3464           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019811,002952: 40,3465           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019812,002953: 40,3466           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019813,002954: 40,3467           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019814,002955: 40,3470           03477                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019815,002956: 40,3471           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019816,002957: 40,3472           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019817,002958: 40,3473           03475                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019818,002959: 40,3474           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019819,002960: 40,3475           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019820,002961: 40,3476           21050                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019821,002962: 40,3477           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019822,002963: 40,3500           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019823,002964: 40,3501           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019824,002965: 40,3502           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019825,002966: 40,3503           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019826,002967: 40,3504           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019827,002968: 
019828,002969: 40,3505                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019829,002970:

Page 451 

019831,002972:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
019832,002973:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019833,002974:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019834,002975:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019835,002976:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
019836,002977: 
019837,002978:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019838,002979:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS -
019839,002980:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
019840,002981: 
019841,002982:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019842,002983:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019843,002984: 
019844,002985:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019845,002986:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019846,002987:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019847,002988:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019848,002989:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019849,002990: 
019850,002991:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019851,002992:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019852,002993:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019853,002994:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019854,002995: 
019855,002996:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019856,002997:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
019857,002998:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019858,002999:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019859,003000:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019860,003001:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019861,003002:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019862,003003: 
019863,003004:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019864,003005:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
019865,003006: 
019866,003007:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019867,003008:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019868,003009: 
019869,003010:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019870,003011:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019871,003012: 
019872,003013:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
019873,003014:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019874,003015:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019875,003016:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
019876,003017:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019877,003018:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
019878,003019:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019879,003020: 
019880,003021:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 452 

019882,003023:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019883,003024:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
019884,003025:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019885,003026:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019886,003027:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
019887,003028:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019888,003029:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019889,003030:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019890,003031:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019891,003032: 
019892,003033:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019893,003034:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019894,003035: 
019895,003036:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
019896,003037: 
019897,003038:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019898,003039:    4154           22007        NVSUB              LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019899,003040:    4155           54123        NVMONOPT           TS       NVTEMP                                
019900,003041:    4156           34736                           CAF      BIT14

019926,003067:    4203           05165                           TC       SUPDXCHZ                              #  DTCB WITH SUPERBIT SWITCHING
019927,003068:

020002,003143:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).
020003,003144: 
020004,003145:    4204                                           SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
020005,003146:    4204                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020006,003147:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
020007,003148:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
020008,003149:    4205           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
020009,003150:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
020010,003151:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
020011,003152: 
020012,003153:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
020013,003154:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020014,003155:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020015,003156:                                                                                                  #                -0              DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
020016,003157:                                                                                                  #                        OR      RESEQUENCE      SET BY VERB 32
020017,003158: 
020018,003159:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
020019,003160:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
020020,003161:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
020021,003162:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020022,003163:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020023,003164:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
020024,003165:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
020025,003166:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
020026,003167:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
020027,003168:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
020028,003169: 
020029,003170:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 455 

020031,003172:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
020032,003173:                                                                                                  #  1)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
020033,003174:                                                                                                  #        EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020034,003175:                                                                                                  #  2)    DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
020035,003176:                                                                                                  #        NVSUBUSY.
020036,003177: 
020037,003178:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
020038,003179:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
020039,003180:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
020040,003181:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
020041,003182:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
020042,003183:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
020043,003184:    4215           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
020044,003185:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
020045,003186: 
020046,003187:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020047,003188: 
020048,003189:    4220           11042        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
020049,003190:    4221           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.

Page 463 

020375,003516:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
020376,003517: 
020377,003518:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
020378,003519:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
020379,003520:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
020380,003521:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
020381,003522: 
020382,003523:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
020383,003524:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1) BY ENDIDLE
020384,003525:                                                                                                  #                2) BY NVSUBUSY
020385,003526:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
020386,003527:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
020387,003528:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
020388,003529:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
020389,003530: 
020390,003531:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
020391,003532:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
020392,003533:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
020393,003534:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
020394,003535:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
020395,003536: 
020396,003537:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
020397,003538:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
020398,003539:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
020399,003540:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020400,003541:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020401,003542: 
020402,003543:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
020403,003544:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
020404,003545:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
020405,003546: 
020406,003547: 
020407,003548:                                                                                                  #  .
020408,003549: 
020409,003550:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
020410,003551:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
020411,003552:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
020412,003553:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
020413,003554: 
020414,003555:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
020415,003556:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
020416,003557:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
020417,003558:                                                                                                  #  1)    DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
020418,003559:                                                                                                  #        IS EXCEEDED.
020419,003560:                                                                                                  #  2)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 464 

020421,003562:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020422,003563: 
020423,003564:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
020424,003565:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
020425,003566:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
020426,003567:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
020427,003568:    4443           10647                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
020428,003569:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
020429,003570: 
020430,003571:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
020431,003572:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
020432,003573: 
020433,003574: 04,2647                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
020434,003575: 04,2647                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020435,003576: 04,2647           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
020436,003577: 04,2650           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
020437,003578: 04,2651           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
020438,003579: 04,2652           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
020439,003580: 04,2653           30001                           CA       L                                     
020440,003581: 04,2654           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
020441,003582: 04,2655           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
020442,003583: 
020443,003584:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
020444,003585:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
020445,003586:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
020446,003587:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
020447,003588:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
020448,003589: 
020449,003590:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
020450,003591:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
020451,003592:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
020452,003593:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
020453,003594:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
020454,003595:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
020455,003596:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
020456,003597:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
020457,003598:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY

020611,003752:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
020612,003753:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
020613,003754:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
020614,003755:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
020615,003756:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
020616,003757:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
020617,003758:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
020618,003759: 
020619,003760: 40,3603                                           SETLOC   DOPROC     +2
